Hello!!!

Welcome to my "How To" where you will create a How To Website!

- Meaning a website that shows you how to make a website that shows you how to make a website... and so on.

What you will need:

- 1 computer (with monitor and has Windows).

- Visual Studio Code.

That's all! Now lets begin the tutorial (Use the < and > buttons to switch pages)

1. Getting Started

- Go to the desktop.

- Create a folder.

- Rename the folder to "How To Website How To".

- Take a screenshot of the folder (Windows + Shift + S).

- Open the image in Snip & Sketch.

- Save the image to the desktop (Ctrl + S).

- Close Snip & Sketch (Always close after you're done with a screenshot and it's saved).

- Rename the image "ss1.png" (or "ss1" if view file extensions is disabled).

2. Making the Proper Files

- Open the folder (When I say "the folder" I'm talking about the "How To Website How To" folder).

- Create another folder in the folder.

- Rename the new folder inside the folder "assets".

- Move all screenshots taken into "assets" folder from now on (Don't forget to move "ss1.png" from the desktop to the "assets" folder).

- Go to the view tab near the top of file explorer.

- In the Show/Hide section; Toggle on "File name extensions".

- Inside of the folder create a new text file using the right click menu; name the file "index.html"; select yes on the pop-up.

- Inside of the folder create a new text file using the right click menu; name the file "style.css"; select yes on the pop-up.

- Inside of the folder create a new text file using the right click menu; name the file "main.js"; select yes on the pop-up.

- Repeat the steps to take a screenshot but take one of the files in the folder (You can save them directly to the assets folder now that it's been created).

- Rename the image to "ss2.png"

3. Getting Ready to Code üò®

- Open Visual Studio Code (vs for short... I am not typing that another 30 times).

- In the file explorer, select "index.html", "style.css", and "main.js"

- Drag and drop the files into vs. (They should appear).

- If prompted with untrusted files alert agree to using the files.

- Click into index.html in the top bar of vs if you're not already inside of it.

- Go to the folder in file explorer and double click open "index.html".

- Repeat the steps to take a screenshot but take one of the top bar of the web browser that should've opened (If it didn't open... well... good luck).

- Rename the image to "ss3.png"

- Click and drag the middle of the top bar of the web browser all the way to the left edge of the screen.

- Let go of the mouse.

- When the grid of applications shows up you must select visual studio code.

- Your screen should now be split-screen between the web browser and vs.

- Click into vs on line 1 of "index.html".

4. Coding üòé

- Add the code between the "*" symbols (Don't add "*" symbols into the actual code, only what is between them):

                 
* 
<!DOCTYPE html>
<html>
    <body>
        
    </body>
    <script src="main.js"></script>
    <link rel="stylesheet" href="style.css">
</html>
*

- After every change to code in vs press (Ctrl + S) to save it.

- To see your changes you can refresh the browser.

- Repeat the steps to take a screenshot but take one of the code that was just added (Include the line numbers in the screenshots).

- Rename the image to "ss4.png".

5. More Coding

Switch to the "style.css" tab in vs (The tabs are near the top of the application).

- Add the following code to "style.css" (Remember don't add in the "*" symbols):

                 
* 
html{background-color: black;
    font-family:system-ui,
     -apple-system,
      BlinkMacSystemFont,
       'Segoe UI',
        Roboto, Oxygen, Ubuntu, Cantarell,
         'Open Sans', 'Helvetica Neue', sans-serif;
         color: lime;
         width: 100%; height: 100%;
         display:grid;
         text-wrap:pretty;
         font-size: x-large;
}
body{
    display: block;
    margin-top:25px;
    margin-left: 20%;
    margin-right: auto;
}
p{width: 50vw; margin-top:auto;}
img{margin-left:5vw;object-fit:scale-down; width:40vw;}
.list{margin-left:35px}
.b{background-color: rgb(20, 20, 20); color: lime;
    font-size: xx-large;
    font-weight:900;
    padding:5%;
    margin: 3px;
    width: 50px;
    border: 0px;
    border-radius: 15px;}
*

- Repeat the steps to take a screenshot but take one of the code that was just added.

- Rename the image to "ss5.png".

6. Moreeee Coding

Switch to the "index.html" tab in vs.

- Add the following code to "index.html" between <body> and </body>:

                 
* 
<div id="page1" name="page">
            <p style="margin-left:20vw" id="header">Hello!!! </p><p>Welcome to my "How To" where you will create a How To Website!</p>
            <p class="list">- Meaning a website that shows you how to make a website that shows you how to make a website... and so on.</p>
            <p>What you will need:</p>
            <div style="margin-bottom: 25px;">
            <p class="list" style="margin-bottom:0px;">- 1 computer (with monitor and has Windows).</p>
            <p class="list" style="margin-bottom:0px;">- Visual Studio Code.</p>
            </div>
            <p>That's all! Now lets begin the tutorial (Use the &lt and &gt buttons to switch pages)</p>
        </div>

*

- Repeat the steps to take a screenshot but take one of the code that was just added.

- Rename the image to "ss6.png".

7. Even MOREEE Coding

Switch to the "index.html" tab in vs.

- Add the following code to "index.html" on line 14 which should be blank:

                 
* 
<div style="display: grid; grid-template-columns: min-content min-content; margin-left:27%;">
            <button class="b" id="leftButton">&lt</button>
            <button class="b" id="rightButton">&gt</button>
            <div hidden>by Jacob Tapper</div>
        </div>
        
*

- Repeat the steps to take a screenshot but take one of the code that was just added.

- Rename the image to "ss7.png".

8. Lotssss of Coding

Switch to the "main.js" tab in vs.

- Add the following code to "main.js":

                 
* 
let page=1;
window.onload = (e)=>{
    hideAllPages();
    document.getElementById("loop").innerHTML=returnString();
    document.getElementById("page1").hidden=false;
    rainbow();
    document.getElementById("leftButton").onclick=(e)=>{
        changePage(false);
    }
    document.getElementById("rightButton").onclick=(e)=>{
        changePage(true);
    }
}
function changePage(right){
    let pages = document.getElementsByName("page");
    (right)?page++:page--;
    if(page==0)page++;
    if(page>pages.length)page--;
    hideAllPages();
    unhidePage();
}
function hideAllPages(){
    document.getElementsByName("page").forEach((i)=>{i.hidden=true;})  
}
function unhidePage(){
    document.getElementById("page"+page).hidden=false;
}
function rainbow(){
    let header = document.getElementById("header").style;
    header.backgroundImage="linear-gradient(to left, blue, blue, blue, blue, blue, red)"
    header.webkitBackgroundClip="text"
    header.color="transparent"
}
function returnString(){
    return `

        if(page==0)page++;
        if(page&amp;gtpages.length)page--;

            <p class="list">- Close Snip & Sketch (Always close after you're done with a screenshot and it's saved).</p>

<div id="page9" name="page">
            <p>8. Lotssss of Coding</p>
            <p class="list">Switch to the "main.js" tab in vs.</p>
            <p class="list">- Add the following code to "main.js":</p>
            <pre class="list">
                <code> 
* 
let page=1;
window.onload = (e)=>{
    hideAllPages();
    document.getElementById("loop").innerHTML=returnString();
    document.getElementById("page1").hidden=false;
    rainbow();
    document.getElementById("leftButton").onclick=(e)=>{
        changePage(false);
    }
    document.getElementById("rightButton").onclick=(e)=>{
        changePage(true);
    }
}
function changePage(right){
    let pages = document.getElementsByName("page");
    (right)?page++:page--;
    if(page==0)page++;
    if(page>pages.length)page--;
    hideAllPages();
    unhidePage();
}
function hideAllPages(){
    document.getElementsByName("page").forEach((i)=>{i.hidden=true;})  
}
function unhidePage(){
    document.getElementById("page"+page).hidden=false;
}
function rainbow(){
    let header = document.getElementById("header").style;
    header.backgroundImage="linear-gradient(to left, blue, blue, blue, blue, blue, red)"
    header.webkitBackgroundClip="text"
    header.color="transparent"
}
function returnString(){
    return `
    * 
    &amp;ltdiv id="page2" name="page"&amp;gt
    &amp;ltp&amp;gt1. Getting Started&amp;lt/p&amp;gt
    &amp;ltp class="list"&amp;gt- Go to the desktop.&amp;lt/p&amp;gt
    &amp;ltp class="list"&amp;gt- Create a folder.&amp;lt/p&amp;gt
    &amp;ltp class="list"&amp;gt- Rename the folder to "How To Website How To".&amp;lt/p&amp;gt
    &amp;ltimg src="assets/ss1.png" style="width: 120px; height: 120px;"&amp;gt
    &amp;ltp class="list"&amp;gt- Take a screenshot of the folder (Windows + Shift + S).&amp;lt/p&amp;gt
    &amp;ltp class="list"&amp;gt- Open the image in Snip &amp; Sketch.&amp;lt/p&amp;gt
    &amp;ltp class="list"&amp;gt- Save the image to the desktop (Ctrl + S).&amp;lt/p&amp;gt
    &amp;ltp class="list"&amp;gt- Close Snip &amp; Sketch (Always close after you're done with a screenshot and it's saved).&amp;lt/p&amp;gt
    &amp;ltp class="list"&amp;gt- Rename the image "ss1.png" (or "ss1" if view file extensions is disabled).&amp;lt/p&amp;gt
&amp;lt/div&amp;gt
&amp;ltdiv id="page3" name="page"&amp;gt
    &amp;ltp&amp;gt2. Making the Proper Files&amp;lt/p&amp;gt
    &amp;ltp class="list"&amp;gt- Open the folder (When I say "the folder" I'm talking about the "How To Website How To" folder).&amp;lt/p&amp;gt
    &amp;ltp class="list"&amp;gt- Create another folder in the folder.&amp;lt/p&amp;gt
    &amp;ltp class="list"&amp;gt- Rename the new folder inside the folder "assets".&amp;lt/p&amp;gt
    &amp;ltp class="list"&amp;gt- Move all screenshots taken into "assets" folder from now on (Don't forget to move "ss1.png" from the desktop to the "assets" folder).&amp;lt/p&amp;gt
    &amp;ltp class="list"&amp;gt- Go to the view tab near the top of file explorer.&amp;lt/p&amp;gt
    &amp;ltp class="list"&amp;gt- In the Show/Hide section; Toggle on "File name extensions".&amp;lt/p&amp;gt
    &amp;ltp class="list"&amp;gt- Inside of the folder create a new text file using the right click menu; name the file "index.html"; select yes on the pop-up.&amp;lt/p&amp;gt
    &amp;ltp class="list"&amp;gt- Inside of the folder create a new text file using the right click menu; name the file "style.css"; select yes on the pop-up.&amp;lt/p&amp;gt
    &amp;ltp class="list"&amp;gt- Inside of the folder create a new text file using the right click menu; name the file "main.js"; select yes on the pop-up.&amp;lt/p&amp;gt
    &amp;ltimg src="assets/ss2.png"&amp;gt
    &amp;ltp class="list"&amp;gt- Repeat the steps to take a screenshot but take one of the files in the folder (You can save them directly to the assets folder now that it's been created).&amp;lt/p&amp;gt
    &amp;ltp class="list"&amp;gt- Rename the image to "ss2.png"&amp;lt/p&amp;gt
&amp;lt/div&amp;gt
&amp;ltdiv id="page4" name="page"&amp;gt
    &amp;ltp&amp;gt3. Getting Ready to Code üò®&amp;lt/p&amp;gt
    &amp;ltp class="list"&amp;gt- Open Visual Studio Code (vs for short... I am not typing that another 30 times).&amp;lt/p&amp;gt
    &amp;ltp class="list"&amp;gt- In the file explorer, select "index.html", "style.css", and "main.js"&amp;lt/p&amp;gt
    &amp;ltp class="list"&amp;gt- Drag and drop the files into vs. (They should appear).&amp;lt/p&amp;gt
    &amp;ltp class="list"&amp;gt- If prompted with untrusted files alert agree to using the files.&amp;lt/p&amp;gt
    &amp;ltp class="list"&amp;gt- Click into index.html in the top bar of vs if you're not already inside of it.&amp;lt/p&amp;gt
    &amp;ltp class="list"&amp;gt- Go to the folder in file explorer and double click open "index.html".&amp;lt/p&amp;gt
    &amp;ltp class="list"&amp;gt- Repeat the steps to take a screenshot but take one of the top bar of the web browser that should've opened (If it didn't open... well... good luck).&amp;lt/p&amp;gt
    &amp;ltp class="list"&amp;gt- Rename the image to "ss3.png"&amp;lt/p&amp;gt
    &amp;ltp class="list"&amp;gt- Click and drag the middle of the top bar of the web browser all the way to the left edge of the screen.&amp;lt/p&amp;gt
    &amp;ltimg src="assets/ss3.png"&amp;gt
    &amp;ltp class="list"&amp;gt- Let go of the mouse.&amp;lt/p&amp;gt
    &amp;ltp class="list"&amp;gt- When the grid of applications shows up you must select visual studio code.&amp;lt/p&amp;gt
    &amp;ltp class="list"&amp;gt- Your screen should now be split-screen between the web browser and vs.&amp;lt/p&amp;gt
    &amp;ltp class="list"&amp;gt- Click into vs on line 1 of "index.html".&amp;lt/p&amp;gt
&amp;lt/div&amp;gt
&amp;ltdiv id="page5" name="page"&amp;gt
    &amp;ltp&amp;gt4. Coding üòé&amp;lt/p&amp;gt
    &amp;ltp class="list"&amp;gt- Add the code between the "*" symbols (Don't add "*" symbols into the actual code, only what is between them):&amp;lt/p&amp;gt
    &amp;ltpre class="list"&amp;gt
        &amp;ltcode&amp;gt 
* 
&amp;amp;lt!DOCTYPE html&amp;amp;gt
&amp;amp;lthtml&amp;amp;gt
&amp;amp;ltbody&amp;amp;gt

&amp;amp;lt/body&amp;amp;gt
&amp;amp;ltscript src="main.js"&amp;amp;gt&amp;amp;lt/script&amp;amp;gt
&amp;amp;ltlink rel="stylesheet" href="style.css"&amp;amp;gt
&amp;amp;lt/html&amp;amp;gt
*
        &amp;lt/code&amp;gt
    &amp;lt/pre&amp;gt
    &amp;ltimg src="assets/ss4.png"&amp;gt
    &amp;ltp class="list"&amp;gt- After every change to code in vs press (Ctrl + S) to save it.&amp;lt/p&amp;gt
    &amp;ltp class="list"&amp;gt- To see your changes you can refresh the browser.&amp;lt/p&amp;gt
    &amp;ltp class="list"&amp;gt- Repeat the steps to take a screenshot but take one of the code that was just added (Include the line numbers in the screenshots).&amp;lt/p&amp;gt
    &amp;ltp class="list"&amp;gt- Rename the image to "ss4.png".&amp;lt/p&amp;gt
&amp;lt/div&amp;gt
&amp;ltdiv id="page6" name="page"&amp;gt
&amp;ltp&amp;gt5. More Coding&amp;lt/p&amp;gt
&amp;ltp class="list"&amp;gtSwitch to the "style.css" tab in vs (The tabs are near the top of the application).&amp;lt/p&amp;gt
&amp;ltp class="list"&amp;gt- Add the following code to "style.css" (Remember don't add in the "*" symbols):&amp;lt/p&amp;gt
&amp;ltpre class="list"&amp;gt
    &amp;ltcode&amp;gt 
* 
html{background-color: black;
font-family:system-ui,
-apple-system,
BlinkMacSystemFont,
'Segoe UI',
Roboto, Oxygen, Ubuntu, Cantarell,
'Open Sans', 'Helvetica Neue', sans-serif;
color: lime;
width: 100%; height: 100%;
display:grid;
text-wrap:pretty;
font-size: x-large;
}
body{
display: block;
margin-top:25px;
margin-left: 20%;
margin-right: auto;
}
p{width: 50vw; margin-top:auto;}
img{margin-left:5vw;object-fit:scale-down; width:40vw;}
.list{margin-left:35px}
.b{background-color: rgb(20, 20, 20); color: lime;
font-size: xx-large;
font-weight:900;
padding:5%;
margin: 3px;
width: 50px;
border: 0px;
border-radius: 15px;}
*
    &amp;lt/code&amp;gt

    &amp;ltp&amp;gt6. Moreeee Coding&amp;lt/p&amp;gt
    &amp;ltp class="list"&amp;gtSwitch to the "index.html" tab in vs.&amp;lt/p&amp;gt
    &amp;ltp class="list"&amp;gt- Add the following code to "index.html" between &amp;ltbody&amp;gt and &amp;lt/body&amp;gt:&amp;lt/p&amp;gt
    &amp;ltpre class="list"&amp;gt

    &amp;amp;ltp style="margin-left:20vw" id="header"&amp;amp;gtHello!!! &amp;amp;lt/p&amp;amp;gt&amp;amp;ltp&amp;amp;gtWelcome to my "How To" where you will create a How To Website!&amp;amp;lt/p&amp;amp;gt
    &amp;amp;ltp class="list"&amp;amp;gt- Meaning a website that shows you how to make a website that shows you how to make a website... and so on.&amp;amp;lt/p&amp;amp;gt
    &amp;amp;ltp&amp;amp;gtWhat you will need:&amp;amp;lt/p&amp;amp;gt

    &amp;ltp&amp;gt8. Lotssss of Coding&amp;lt/p&amp;gt
    &amp;ltp class="list"&amp;gtSwitch to the "main.js" tab in vs.&amp;lt/p&amp;gt
    &amp;ltp class="list"&amp;gt- Add the following code to "main.js":&amp;lt/p&amp;gt
    &amp;ltpre class="list"&amp;gt
        &amp;ltcode&amp;gt 
* 
let page=1;
window.onload = (e)=&amp;gt{
hideAllPages();
document.getElementById("page1").hidden=false;
rainbow();
document.getElementById("leftButton").onclick=(e)=&amp;gt{
changePage(false);
}
document.getElementById("rightButton").onclick=(e)=&amp;gt{
changePage(true);
}
}
function changePage(right){
let pages = document.getElementsByName("page");
(right)?page++:page--;
if(page==0)page++;
if(page&amp;gtpages.length)page--;
hideAllPages();
unhidePage();
}
function hideAllPages(){
document.getElementsByName("page").forEach((i)=&amp;gt{i.hidden=true;})  
}
function unhidePage(){
document.getElementById("page"+page).hidden=false;
}
function rainbow(){
let header = document.getElementById("header").style;
header.backgroundImage="linear-gradient(to left, blue, blue, blue, blue, blue, red)"
header.webkitBackgroundClip="text"
header.color="transparent"
}

*
        &amp;lt/code&amp;gt
